namespace = daoyu_edit_planet
country_event = {
	id = daoyu_edit_planet.1
	title = daoyu_edit_planet
	desc = daoyu_target_planet_desc
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	location = event_target:daoyu_target_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = daoyu_special_project_select_target#选择星球
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_target_planet
		set_global_flag = daoyu_edit_planet_special_project
		daoyu_special_project_select_target = yes
		custom_tooltip = daoyu_pause_game
	}
	option = {
		name = planet_devastation#行星破坏度
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { planet_devastation > 0 } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { add_planet_devastation = -100 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = effect_every_ambient_object#所有环境物体
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { any_system_ambient_object = { daoyu_ambient_object_trigger = yes } } }
		every_system_ambient_object = { limit = { daoyu_ambient_object_trigger = yes } destroy_ambient_object = this }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_spawn_planet#创建星球
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_can_spawn_planets_trigger = yes } }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.5 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_planet#移除行星
		trigger = { or = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { is_colony = no is_star = no } event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { has_astral_rift = yes } } }
		allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = PLANET_HAS_NOT_MOON or = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_has_moon_trigger = no } event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { has_astral_rift = yes } } } }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.3 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = REMOVE_MODIFIER
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_has_planet_modifiers_trigger = yes } }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_remove_planet_modifiers.1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = BUILD_STARBASE_STATION_ORDER#建造恒星基地
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { not = { exists = starbase } } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { create_starbase = { size = starbase_outpost owner = root } }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_upgrade_starbase#升级恒星基地
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { exists = starbase starbase = { not = { has_starbase_size = starbase_citadel } } } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system.starbase = {
			if = { limit = { has_starbase_size = starbase_outpost } set_starbase_size = starbase_starport }
			else_if = { limit = { has_starbase_size = starbase_starport } if = { limit = { root = { has_technology = tech_starbase_3 } } set_starbase_size = starbase_starhold } else = { set_global_flag = daoyu_missing_technology } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_starbase_size = starbase_starhold } if = { limit = { root = { has_technology = tech_starbase_4 } } set_starbase_size = starbase_starfortress } else = { set_global_flag = daoyu_missing_technology } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_starbase_size = starbase_starfortress } if = { limit = { root = { has_technology = tech_starbase_5 } } set_starbase_size = starbase_citadel } else = { set_global_flag = daoyu_missing_technology } }
		}
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_missing_technology } remove_global_flag = daoyu_missing_technology country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.2 } } else = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = PLANET_SIZE#行星规模
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { or = { daoyu_common_habitable_planets_trigger = yes has_astral_planes_dlc = yes not = { is_planet_class = pc_astral_scar } } } }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.100 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = PLANETVIEW_PLANET_CLASS#行星类型
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { or = { has_astral_planes_dlc = yes not = { is_planet_class = pc_astral_scar } } is_colony = no } }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.110 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = PLANETVIEW_PLANET_RESOURCES#行星资源
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { is_colony = no } }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.120 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = fa_colonized_planet#已殖民星球
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { is_colony = yes } }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.190 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = MEGASTRUCTURE#巨型结构
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.200 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_spawn_system#创建星系
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.250 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_edit_planet_in_progress } }
		default_hide_option = yes
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_target_planet
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.100 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CLOSE
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_edit_planet_in_progress }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_edit_planet_in_progress
		default_hide_option = yes
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_target_planet
	}
}
#升级恒星基地
country_event = {
	id = daoyu_edit_planet.2
	title = daoyu_upgrade_starbase
	desc = MISSING_TECHNOLOGY#缺少科技
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	location = event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system.starbase
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = tech_starbase_3
		trigger = { not = { has_technology = tech_starbase_3 } event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system.starbase = { has_starbase_size = starbase_starport } }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_starbase_3 MESSAGE = no }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system.starbase = { set_starbase_size = starbase_starhold }
	}
	option = {
		name = tech_starbase_4
		trigger = { not = { has_technology = tech_starbase_4 } event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system.starbase = { has_starbase_size = starbase_starhold } }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_starbase_4 MESSAGE = no }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system.starbase = { set_starbase_size = starbase_starfortress }
	}
	option = {
		name = tech_starbase_5
		trigger = { not = { has_technology = tech_starbase_5 } event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system.starbase = { has_starbase_size = starbase_starfortress } }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_starbase_5 MESSAGE = no }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system.starbase = { set_starbase_size = starbase_citadel }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
	after = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 } } }
}
#移除行星
country_event = {
	id = daoyu_edit_planet.3
	title = daoyu_remove_planet
	desc = daoyu_target_planet_desc
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	location = event_target:daoyu_target_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#确认
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { is_colony = no is_star = no } }
		allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = PLANET_HAS_NOT_MOON event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_has_moon_trigger = no } } }
		custom_tooltip = daoyu_remove_planet_tt
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { remove_planet = yes }
		if = { limit = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_has_ring } } remove_global_flag = daoyu_edit_planet_in_progress clear_global_event_target = daoyu_target_planet }
		else = { event_target:daoyu_prev_target_planet = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_planet } clear_global_event_target = daoyu_prev_target_planet hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.5 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ASTRAL_RIFT#星界裂隙
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { has_astral_rift = yes } }
		allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = daoyu_cooldown_1 not = { has_country_flag = daoyu_random_astral_rift } } }
		random_astral_rift = { limit = { solar_system = { is_same_value = event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system } } destroy_astral_rift = this }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_spawn_planet } }
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NO_THANKS#不用了
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_spawn_planet }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_spawn_planet
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_prev_target_planet
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 } }
	}
}
#创建星球
country_event = {
	id = daoyu_edit_planet.5
	title = daoyu_spawn_planet#预计位置
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			text = daoyu_target_planet_desc
			text = daoyu_orbit_distance_offset_show
			text = daoyu_orbit_angle_offset_show
			success_text = { text = HAS_RING has_global_flag = daoyu_has_ring }
			success_text = { text = HAS_NOT_RING not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_has_ring } }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	location = event_target:daoyu_target_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_orbit_distance_offset VALUE_IF_CREATED = 100 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_orbit_angle_offset VALUE_IF_CREATED = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = SETTINGS_RESET#重置
		set_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance_offset value = 100 }
		set_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle_offset value = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_add_50
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance_offset value = 50 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_add_10
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance_offset value = 10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_sub_10
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance_offset value = -10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_sub_50
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance_offset value = -50 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_angle_add_30
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle_offset value = 30 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_angle_sub_30
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle_offset value = -30 }
	}
	option = {
		name = HAS_RING
		allow = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_has_ring } }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_has_ring
	}
	option = {
		name = HAS_NOT_RING
		allow = { has_global_flag = daoyu_has_ring }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_has_ring
	}
	option = {
		name = CREATE#创建
		set_global_flag = daoyu_spawn_planet
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
		daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_orbit_distance_offset VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_orbit_angle_offset WHAT = pc_barren }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.3 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_spawn_planet
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 } }
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back } else = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.5 } }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle value >= 360 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle value = -360 } }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle value < 0 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle value = 360 } }
		}
	}
}
#行星规模
country_event = {
	id = daoyu_edit_planet.100
	title = PLANET_SIZE
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			text = daoyu_target_planet_desc
			text = daoyu_target_planet_size_desc
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = event_target:daoyu_target_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { export_trigger_value_to_variable = { trigger = planet_size variable = daoyu_planet_size_var } } }
	option = {
		name = 5
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { set_planet_size = 5 }
	}
	option = {
		name = 10
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { set_planet_size = 10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = 15
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { set_planet_size = 15 }
	}
	option = {
		name = 20
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { set_planet_size = 20 }
	}
	option = {
		name = 25
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { set_planet_size = 25 }
	}
	option = {
		name = 30
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { set_planet_size = 30 }
	}
	option = {
		name = +1
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { change_planet_size = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = -1
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { change_planet_size = -1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = d_gravity_storm_1_districts
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { has_cosmic_storms_dlc = yes daoyu_common_habitable_planets_trigger = yes } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { add_deposit = d_gravity_storm_1_districts }
	}
	option = {
		name = colonizer
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_common_habitable_planets_trigger = yes is_colony = no not = { any_fleet_in_orbit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer } } } }
		create_fleet = { effect = { set_owner = root create_ship = { random_existing_design = colonizer colonizer_species = root.owner_main_species graphical_culture = root } set_location = event_target:daoyu_target_planet } }
	}
	option = {
		name = district_generator#发电区划
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_common_habitable_planets_trigger = yes } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = {
			if = { limit = { not = { has_modifier = ultra_rich } } add_modifier = { modifier = hazardous_weather days = -1 } }
			if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_arctic is_planet_class = pc_tundra is_planet_class = pc_savannah is_planet_class = pc_desert is_planet_class = pc_arid } } add_deposit = d_geothermal_vent }
			if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_gaia is_planet_class = pc_relic is_planet_class = pc_ocean is_planet_class = pc_nuked is_planet_class = pc_machine } } add_deposit = d_underwater_vent }
			if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_tropical is_planet_class = pc_alpine is_planet_class = pc_continental is_planet_class = pc_hive } } add_deposit = d_tempestous_mountain }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = district_mining#采矿区划
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_common_habitable_planets_trigger = yes } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = {
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = mineral_poor } remove_modifier = mineral_poor }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_modifier = ultra_rich } } add_modifier = { modifier = ultra_rich days = -1 } }
			if = { limit = { has_deposit = d_empty_quarry } while = { count = 5 remove_deposit = d_empty_quarry } }
			if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_continental is_planet_class = pc_desert is_planet_class = pc_alpine is_planet_class = pc_arctic is_planet_class = pc_gaia is_planet_class = pc_machine } } add_deposit = d_rich_mountain }
			if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_ocean is_planet_class = pc_arctic is_planet_class = pc_arid is_planet_class = pc_tundra is_planet_class = pc_nuked is_planet_class = pc_relic } } add_deposit = d_ore_rich_caverns }
			if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_tropical is_planet_class = pc_savannah is_planet_class = pc_hive } } add_deposit = d_prosperous_mesa }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = district_farming#农业区划
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_common_habitable_planets_trigger = yes } }
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { nor = { is_planet_class = pc_relic is_planet_class = pc_machine } } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = {
			if = { limit = { not = { has_modifier = lush_planet } } add_modifier = { modifier = lush_planet days = -1 } }
			if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_continental is_planet_class = pc_savannah } } add_deposit = d_black_soil }
			if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_gaia is_planet_class = pc_ocean } } add_deposit = d_teeming_reef }
			if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_arid is_planet_class = pc_desert is_planet_class = pc_tropical } } add_deposit = d_tropical_island }
			if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_tundra is_planet_class = pc_arctic is_planet_class = pc_alpine } } add_deposit = d_fungal_forest }
			if = { limit = { is_planet_class = pc_nuked } add_deposit = d_junk_canals }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = col_research#科技星球
		trigger = { has_distar = yes event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { nor = { has_modifier = daoyu_enigmatic_cache_in_orbit has_deposit = d_valley_of_zanaam has_deposit = d_former_relic_world has_deposit = d_central_spire } } }
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { has_anomaly = no } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = {
			add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_enigmatic_cache_in_orbit day = -1 }
			clear_deposits = yes
			if = { limit = { not = { is_planet_class = pc_relic } } change_pc = pc_relic }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = holy_planet } remove_modifier = holy_planet solar_system = { random_system_ambient_object = { limit = { is_ambient_object_type = consecrated_planet_stage_3_object } destroy_ambient_object = this } } }
			hidden_effect = {
				add_deposit = d_relic_dense_ruins#密集废墟
				add_deposit = d_central_spire#中央尖塔
				add_deposit = d_former_relic_world#前遗落星球
				add_deposit = d_valley_of_zanaam#扎娜姆之谷
				add_deposit = d_mutant_landfill#突变体填埋场
				add_deposit = d_ancient_bombardment_craters#远古轰炸弹坑
				add_deposit = d_ancient_battlefield#古战场
				add_deposit = d_irradiated_ruins#辐射废墟
				add_deposit = d_ancient_particle_accelerator#远古粒子加速器
				add_deposit = d_underground_vault#地下避难所
				add_deposit = d_flooded_mounds#被淹没的丘穴
				add_deposit = d_wetware_computer#湿体电脑
				prevent_anomaly = yes
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { is_gestalt = no event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { not = { has_modifier = colonial_spirit_mod } } } event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { remove_modifier = colonial_spirit_gestalt_mod add_modifier = { modifier = colonial_spirit_mod day = -1 } } }
		if = { limit = { is_gestalt = no event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { not = { has_modifier = prosp_uni_mod } } } event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { remove_modifier = prosp_uni_mod_gestalt add_modifier = { modifier = prosp_uni_mod day = -1 } } }
		if = { limit = { is_gestalt = yes event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { not = { has_modifier = colonial_spirit_gestalt_mod } } } event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { remove_modifier = colonial_spirit_mod add_modifier = { modifier = colonial_spirit_gestalt_mod day = -1 } } }
		if = { limit = { is_gestalt = yes event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { not = { has_modifier = prosp_uni_mod_gestalt } } } event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { remove_modifier = prosp_uni_mod add_modifier = { modifier = prosp_uni_mod_gestalt day = -1 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = SETTINGS_RESET#重置
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_common_habitable_planets_trigger = yes } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = {
			reroll_deposits = yes reroll_planet_modifiers = yes
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_enigmatic_cache_in_orbit } remove_modifier = daoyu_enigmatic_cache_in_orbit }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = colonial_spirit_mod } remove_modifier = colonial_spirit_mod }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = prosp_uni_mod } remove_modifier = prosp_uni_mod }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = colonial_spirit_gestalt_mod } remove_modifier = colonial_spirit_gestalt_mod }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = prosp_uni_mod_gestalt } remove_modifier = prosp_uni_mod_gestalt }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CLEAR#清除
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_common_habitable_planets_trigger = yes } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { clear_deposits = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
		hidden_effect = { clear_variable = daoyu_planet_size_var country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 } }
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back } else = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.100 } } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = daoyu_edit_planet.120
	title = PLANETVIEW_PLANET_RESOURCES
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = { text = daoyu_all_x1 has_global_flag = daoyu_all_x1 }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_all_x5 has_global_flag = daoyu_all_x5 }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_all_x10 has_global_flag = daoyu_all_x10 }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_all_x100 has_global_flag = daoyu_all_x100 }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_all_x1000 has_global_flag = daoyu_all_x1000 }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = event_target:daoyu_target_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { set_global_flag = daoyu_refresh }
	option = {
		name = daoyu_set_multiple#设置倍率
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_refresh
		set_global_flag = daoyu_from_event_edit_planet_120
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_common.1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = BUILD_MINING_STATION_ORDER#建造开采站
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_can_build_mining_station_trigger = yes } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { create_mining_station = { owner = root } }
	}
	option = {
		name = BUILD_RESEARCH_STATION_ORDER#建造研究站
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { daoyu_can_build_research_station_trigger = yes } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { create_research_station = { owner = root } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_clear_deposits
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { or = { has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station has_deposit_for = shipclass_mining_station } } }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_refresh
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.129 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = d_energy_10
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { not = { has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station } } }
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { not = { is_planet_class = pc_astral_scar } } }
		daoyu_set_planet_resource_effect = { DEPOSIT = d_energy_10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = d_minerals_10
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { not = { has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station } } }
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { not = { is_planet_class = pc_astral_scar } } }
		daoyu_set_planet_resource_effect = { DEPOSIT = d_minerals_10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = d_food_10
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { not = { has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station } } }
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { not = { is_planet_class = pc_astral_scar } } }
		daoyu_set_planet_resource_effect = { DEPOSIT = d_food_10 }
	}
	option = {

		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_planet = { not = { has_deposit_for = shipclass_research_station } } }

			clear_deposits = yes

	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.120 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = daoyu_edit_planet.205
	title = wrecked_fleet_poi_title#预计位置
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			text = daoyu_target_system_desc
			text = daoyu_orbit_distance_show
			text = daoyu_orbit_angle_show
			success_text = { text = gateway_ruined has_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_ruined }
			success_text = { text = lgate_base has_global_flag = daoyu_lgate_base }
			success_text = { text = gateway_final has_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_final }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	location = event_target:daoyu_target_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_orbit_distance VALUE_IF_CREATED = 250 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_orbit_angle VALUE_IF_CREATED = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = SETTINGS_RESET#重置
		set_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance value = 150 }
		set_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle value = 0 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_add_50
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance value = 50 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_add_10
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance value = 10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_sub_10
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance value = -10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_sub_50
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance value = -50 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_angle_add_30
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle value = 30 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_angle_sub_30
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle value = -30 }
	}
	option = {
		name = BUILD#建造
		set_global_flag = daoyu_spawn_megastructure
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_ruined } daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_orbit_distance VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_orbit_angle WHAT = gateway_ruined } }
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_lgate_base } daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_orbit_distance VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_orbit_angle WHAT = lgate_base } }
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_final } daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_orbit_distance VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_orbit_angle WHAT = gateway_0 } }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.206 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_lgate_base
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_ruined
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_final
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_spawn_megastructure
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.200 } }
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back } else = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.205 } }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance value > 400 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_distance value = -400 } }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle value >= 360 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle value = -360 } }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle value < 0 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_orbit_angle value = 360 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = daoyu_edit_planet.206
	title = STARBASE_DISMANTLE_COMPONENT_DIALOG_TITLE#是否拆解
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			text = daoyu_target_system_desc
			text = daoyu_orbit_distance_show
			text = daoyu_orbit_angle_show
			success_text = { text = gateway_ruined has_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_ruined }
			success_text = { text = lgate_base has_global_flag = daoyu_lgate_base }
			success_text = { text = gateway_final has_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_final }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	location = event_target:daoyu_megastructure
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = STARBASE_DISMANTLE_LABEL#拆解
		event_target:daoyu_megastructure = { remove_megastructure = this }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.205 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = NO_THANKS#不用了
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.200 } }
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_lgate_base }
			event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { set_star_flag = daoyu_lgate_base set_star_flag = lgate }
			if = { limit = { nor = { has_country_flag = encountered_first_lgate has_event_chain = "l_cluster_chain" } } country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.208 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_ruined }
			event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { set_star_flag = daoyu_gateway_ruined set_star_flag = abandoned_gateway }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_country_flag = encountered_first_gateway } } country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.207 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_final }
			event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { set_star_flag = daoyu_gateway_final }
			event_target:daoyu_megastructure = { upgrade_megastructure_to = gateway_final finish_upgrade = yes }
		}
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_lgate_base
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_ruined
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_gateway_final
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_spawn_megastructure
	}
}

		event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { save_event_target_as = gateway_system }
		set_country_flag = encountered_first_gateway
		add_seen_bypass_type = gateway
	}
	option = { name = INTRIGUING }

country_event = {
	id = daoyu_edit_planet.208
	title = "apoc.1.name"
	desc = { text = apoc.3.desc trigger = { not = { has_country_flag = encountered_first_gateway } } }
	desc = { text = apoc.3.b.desc trigger = { has_country_flag = encountered_first_gateway } }
	picture = GFX_evt_l-gateway
	show_sound = event_radio_chatter
	location = event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { save_event_target_as = gateway_system }
		set_country_flag = encountered_first_lgate
	}
	option = { name = INTRIGUING start_lcluster_chain = yes }
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:daoyu_target_planet.solar_system = { random_system_planet = { limit = { is_star = no has_anomaly = no } add_anomaly = { category = transmitter_cat } } }
			if = {
				limit = { any_planet_within_border = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant has_any_strategic_resource = no has_anomaly = no } }
				random_planet_within_border = { limit = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant has_any_strategic_resource = no has_anomaly = no } add_anomaly = { category = DISTAR_MEDGAS_CAT } }
			}
			else = {
				every_system_within_border = {
					limit = { any_neighbor_system = { not = { exists = owner } any_system_planet = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant has_any_strategic_resource = no has_anomaly = no } } }
					random_galaxy_planet = { limit = { is_planet_class = pc_gas_giant has_any_strategic_resource = no has_anomaly = no solar_system = { any_neighbor_system = { is_owned_by = root } } } add_anomaly = { category = DISTAR_MEDGAS_CAT } }
				}
			}
			while = {
				count = 5
				if = { limit = { any_planet_within_border = { is_planet_class = pc_barren } } random_planet_within_border = { limit = { is_planet_class = pc_barren } add_anomaly = { category = AIANOM_CLUE_CAT } } }
				else_if = {
					limit = { any_galaxy_planet = { is_planet_class = pc_barren solar_system = { not = { exists = owner } any_neighbor_system = { is_owned_by = root } } } }
					random_galaxy_planet = { limit = { is_planet_class = pc_barren solar_system = { not = { exists = owner } any_neighbor_system = { is_owned_by = root } } } add_anomaly = { category = AIANOM_CLUE_CAT } }
				}
				else = { random_galaxy_planet = { limit = { is_planet_class = pc_barren solar_system = { not = { exists = owner } any_system = { distance = { source = prev max_jumps = 3 } is_owned_by = root } } } add_anomaly = { category = AIANOM_CLUE_CAT } } }
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = daoyu_spawn_system#创建星系

			text = daoyu_target_system_desc
			text = daoyu_distance_show
			text = daoyu_angle_show

			success_text = { text = daoyu_no_hyperlane has_global_flag = daoyu_no_hyperlane }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_create_starbase has_global_flag = daoyu_create_starbase }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_no_starbase has_global_flag = daoyu_no_starbase }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	location = event_target:daoyu_target_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_distance VALUE_IF_CREATED = 30 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_angle VALUE_IF_CREATED = 0 }
		if = { limit = { nor = { has_global_flag = daoyu_yes_hyperlane has_global_flag = daoyu_no_hyperlane } } set_global_flag = daoyu_yes_hyperlane }
		if = { limit = { nor = { has_global_flag = daoyu_create_starbase has_global_flag = daoyu_no_starbase } } set_global_flag = daoyu_create_starbase }
	}
	option = {
		name = SETTINGS#设置

	}

			50 = { daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_distance VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_angle WHAT = custom_starting_init_05 } }

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_binary_star_system#双星系统
		random_list = {
			50 = { daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_distance VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_angle WHAT = custom_starting_init_03 } }
			50 = { daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_distance VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_angle WHAT = custom_starting_init_04 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_trinary_star_system#三星系统
		random_list = {
			50 = { daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_distance VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_angle WHAT = custom_starting_init_01 } }
			50 = { daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_distance VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_angle WHAT = custom_starting_init_02 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = utopia.2016.name#废弃的环形世界
		trigger = { has_utopia = yes }
		daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_distance VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_angle WHAT = daoyu_only_star_01 }
		event_target:daoyu_new_initializer = { set_star_flag = ruined_ring_system daoyu_dyson_sphere_effcet = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = dyson_sphere_ruined#废弃的戴森球
		trigger = { has_utopia = yes }
		daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_distance VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_angle WHAT = daoyu_only_star_01 }

	}
	option = {
		name = matter_decompressor_ruined#被毁的物质解压器
		trigger = { has_utopia = yes }
		daoyu_spawn = { DISTANCE_TYPE = daoyu_distance VALUE_TYPE = daoyu_angle WHAT = daoyu_only_star_01 }

		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_new_initializer

			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back }

	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_add_50
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_distance value = 50 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_add_10
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_distance value = 10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_sub_10
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_distance value = -10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_distance_sub_50
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_distance value = -50 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_angle_add_30
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_angle value = 30 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_angle_sub_30
		change_variable = { which = daoyu_angle value = -30 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_yes_hyperlane
		allow = { has_global_flag = daoyu_no_hyperlane }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_no_hyperlane
		set_global_flag = daoyu_yes_hyperlane
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_no_hyperlane
		allow = { has_global_flag = daoyu_yes_hyperlane }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_yes_hyperlane
		set_global_flag = daoyu_no_hyperlane
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_starbase
		allow = { has_global_flag = daoyu_no_starbase }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_no_starbase
		set_global_flag = daoyu_create_starbase
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_no_starbase
		allow = { has_global_flag = daoyu_create_starbase }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_create_starbase
		set_global_flag = daoyu_no_starbase
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_special_system } remove_global_flag = daoyu_special_system country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.260 } }
			else = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.251 } }
		}
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back } else = { country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.252 } }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_distance value > 400 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_distance value = -400 } }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_angle value >= 360 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_angle value = -360 } }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_angle value < 0 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_angle value = 360 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = daoyu_target_planet_desc
	desc = daoyu_cheat_desc

	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = fromfrom
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { fromfrom = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_planet } }
	option = {
		name = daoyu_edit_planet#编辑星球
		set_global_flag = daoyu_edit_planet_in_progress
		country_event = { id = daoyu_edit_planet.1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_gain_fleet#获得舰队
		set_global_flag = daoyu_gain_fleet_from_planet remove_global_flag = daoyu_gain_fleet
		fromfrom = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_gain_fleet_location }
		country_event = { id = daoyu.130 }
	}
	option = {
		name = concept_hyperlanes#超空间航道
		set_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map
		fromfrom.solar_system = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_point_A }
		country_event = { id = daoyu.110 }
	}
	option = {
		name = CLOSE
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
}

	desc = daoyu_cheat_desc

		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_noxious_swamp MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_quicksand_basin MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_deep_sinkhole MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_toxic_kelp MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_dense_jungle MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_dangerous_wildlife MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_volcano MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_mountain_range MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_physics_1 MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_physics_2 MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_physics_3 MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_society_1 MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_society_2 MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_society_3 MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_engineering_1 MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_engineering_2 MESSAGE = no }
		give_tech_no_error_effect = { TECH = tech_engineering_3 MESSAGE = no }
		hidden_effect = {
			owner_main_species = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_species }
			daoyu_target_species_remove_negative_traits = yes
			change_dominant_species = { species = event_target:daoyu_target_species change_all = yes }
			random_owned_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_military exists = leader } leader = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_initial_commander unassign_leader = this } destroy_fleet = this }
			random_owned_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship exists = leader leader = { has_skill < 10 } } leader = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_initial_scientist unassign_leader = this } destroy_fleet = this }
			every_owned_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor } destroy_fleet = this }
			every_owned_leader = {
				daoyu_remove_all_negative_traits = yes
				set_leader_flag = immune_to_negative_traits
				change_species = event_target:daoyu_target_species
				if = { limit = { leader_class = commander daoyu_subclass_commander_trigger = no is_ruler = yes } add_trait = { trait = subclass_commander_councilor show_message = no } }
				if = { limit = { is_councilor = yes leader_class = commander daoyu_subclass_commander_trigger = no is_gestalt = yes } add_trait = { trait = subclass_commander_councilor show_message = no } }
				if = { limit = { is_councilor = yes leader_class = commander daoyu_subclass_commander_trigger = no is_gestalt = no } add_trait = { trait = subclass_commander_admiral show_message = no } }
				if = { limit = { is_councilor = yes leader_class = official daoyu_subclass_official_trigger = no } add_trait = { trait = subclass_official_economy_councilor show_message = no } }
				if = { limit = { is_councilor = yes leader_class = scientist daoyu_subclass_scientist_trigger = no } add_trait = { trait = subclass_scientist_councilor show_message = no } }
				if = {
					limit = { has_paragon_dlc = yes is_councilor = yes }
					if = { limit = { has_trait = subclass_commander_councilor } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_maven_of_war show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_armada_logistician_3 show_message = no } }
					if = { limit = { has_trait = subclass_commander_admiral } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_master_gunner show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_artillerist_3 show_message = no } }
					if = { limit = { has_trait = subclass_official_economy_councilor } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_supreme_organizer show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = trait_ruler_architectural_sense_3 show_message = no } }
					if = { limit = { has_trait = subclass_scientist_councilor } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_great_researcher show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_brilliant_shipwright show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = trait_ruler_expansionist_3 show_message = no } }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_paragon_dlc = yes is_councilor = no is_gestalt = yes }
					if = { limit = { leader_class = commander daoyu_subclass_commander_trigger = no } add_trait = { trait = subclass_commander_admiral show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_master_gunner show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_artillerist_3 show_message = no } }
					if = { limit = { leader_class = official daoyu_subclass_official_trigger = no } add_trait = { trait = subclass_official_governor show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_galvanizer show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_pop_focused_3 show_message = no } }
					if = { limit = { leader_class = scientist daoyu_subclass_scientist_trigger = no } add_trait = { trait = subclass_scientist_explorer show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_xeno_cataloger show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_observant_3 show_message = no } }
				}
				if = { limit = { has_trait = subclass_scientist_councilor } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_collaborator_3 show_message = no } }
				if = { limit = { is_ruler = no } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_bureaucrat_2 show_message = no } add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_environmental_engineer_2 show_message = no } }
				if = { limit = { or = { is_gestalt = no is_councilor = yes } not = { has_trait = leader_trait_politician_2 } } remove_trait = leader_trait_politician add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_politician_2 show_message = no } }
				if = { limit = { not = { has_trait = leader_trait_eager_2 } } remove_trait = leader_trait_eager add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_eager_2 show_message = no } }
				if = { limit = { has_skill < 3 } set_skill = 3 }
			}
			every_pool_leader = {
				daoyu_remove_all_negative_traits = yes
				set_leader_flag = immune_to_negative_traits
				change_species = event_target:daoyu_target_species
				if = { limit = { not = { has_trait = leader_trait_eager_2 } } remove_trait = leader_trait_eager add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_eager_2 show_message = no } }
				if = { limit = { is_gestalt = no not = { has_trait = leader_trait_politician_2 } } remove_trait = leader_trait_politician add_trait = { trait = leader_trait_politician_2 show_message = no } }
				if = { limit = { has_skill < 3 } set_skill = 3 }
			}
			create_fleet = {
				name = theimperialfleet
				effect = {
					while = { count = 5 if = { limit = { has_first_contact_dlc = yes } create_ship = { name = random design = "daoyu_design_cloaking_corvette" graphical_culture = root } } else = { create_ship = { name = random design = "daoyu_design_corvette" graphical_culture = root } } }
					set_owner = root set_fleet_stance = evasive set_location = root.capital_scope assign_leader = event_target:daoyu_initial_commander
				}
			}
			clear_global_event_target = daoyu_initial_commander
			create_fleet = {
				name = subclass_scientist_explorer
				effect = {
					if = { limit = { has_first_contact_dlc = yes } create_ship = { name = random design = "daoyu_design_cloaking_science" graphical_culture = root } }
					else = { create_ship = { name = random design = "daoyu_design_science" graphical_culture = root } }
					set_owner = root set_fleet_stance = evasive set_location = root.capital_scope assign_leader = event_target:daoyu_initial_scientist
					if = { limit = { has_first_contact_dlc = yes } set_cloaking_active = yes }
				}
			}
			clear_global_event_target = daoyu_initial_scientist
			while = { count = 2 create_fleet = { effect = { set_owner = root create_ship = { name = random design = "daoyu_design_constructor" } set_fleet_stance = evasive set_location = root.capital_scope } } }
			every_planet_within_border = {
				if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_asteroid is_planet_class = pc_ice_asteroid is_planet_class = pc_molten } } add_deposit = d_alloys_5 }
				if = { limit = { daoyu_has_energy_deposit = yes } add_deposit = d_energy_10 }
				if = { limit = { daoyu_has_minerals_deposit = yes } add_deposit = d_minerals_10 }
				if = { limit = { daoyu_has_alloys_deposit = yes } add_deposit = d_alloys_25 }
				if = { limit = { daoyu_has_society_deposit = yes } add_deposit = society_10 }
				if = { limit = { daoyu_has_physics_deposit = yes } add_deposit = d_physics_10 }
				if = { limit = { daoyu_has_engineering_deposit = yes } add_deposit = d_engineering_10 }
				if = { limit = { daoyu_can_build_mining_station_trigger = yes } create_mining_station = { owner = root } }
				if = { limit = { daoyu_can_build_research_station_trigger = yes } create_research_station = { owner = root } }
			}
			every_system = {
				limit = { nor = { is_same_value = root.capital_scope.solar_system has_hyperlane_to = root.capital_scope.solar_system } distance = { source = root.capital_scope.solar_system type = euclidean min_distance >= 0 max_distance <= 30 } }
				add_hyperlane = { from = this to = root.capital_scope.solar_system }
			}
			root.capital_scope.solar_system = {
				every_neighbor_system = {
					limit = { has_owner = no }
					every_system_planet = {
						if = { limit = { or = { is_planet_class = pc_asteroid is_planet_class = pc_ice_asteroid is_planet_class = pc_molten } } add_deposit = d_alloys_5 }
						if = { limit = { daoyu_has_energy_deposit = yes } while = { count = 3 add_deposit = d_energy_10 } }
						if = { limit = { daoyu_has_minerals_deposit = yes } while = { count = 3 add_deposit = d_minerals_10 } }
						if = { limit = { daoyu_has_alloys_deposit = yes } add_deposit = d_alloys_25 }
						if = { limit = { daoyu_has_society_deposit = yes } while = { count = 3 add_deposit = society_10 } }
						if = { limit = { daoyu_has_physics_deposit = yes } while = { count = 3 add_deposit = d_physics_10 } }
						if = { limit = { daoyu_has_engineering_deposit = yes } while = { count = 3 add_deposit = d_engineering_10 } }
					}
				}
				while = {
					count = 3
					random_neighbor_system = {
						limit = { has_owner = no }
						random_system_planet = {
							limit = { is_star = yes }
							root = { daoyu_create_scientist = yes }
							if = { limit = { has_first_contact_dlc = no } create_fleet = { effect = { set_owner = root create_ship = { name = random design = "daoyu_design_science" } set_fleet_stance = evasive set_location = prev assign_leader = last_created_leader } } }
							else = { create_fleet = { effect = { set_owner = root create_ship = { name = random design = "daoyu_design_cloaking_science" } set_fleet_stance = evasive set_location = prev assign_leader = last_created_leader set_cloaking_active = yes } } }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			create_fleet = { effect = { set_owner = root create_ship = { random_existing_design = colonizer colonizer_species = event_target:daoyu_target_species graphical_culture = root } set_location = root.capital_scope } }
			if = {
				limit = { any_country = { not = { is_same_value = root } owner_main_species = { is_same_species = event_target:daoyu_target_species } } }
				root.capital_scope.solar_system = {
					spawn_natural_wormhole = { bypass_type = wormhole random_pos = no orbit_angle = 360 }
					random_system = {
						limit = { any_system_planet = { is_capital = yes owner = { is_ai = yes owner_main_species = { is_same_species = event_target:daoyu_target_species } } } }
						spawn_natural_wormhole = { bypass_type = wormhole random_pos = no orbit_angle = 270 } link_wormholes = prev
					}
				}
			}
			clear_global_event_target = daoyu_target_species
		}
		if = { limit = { is_gestalt = no has_paragon_dlc = yes or = { has_unlocked_council_positions < 4 and = { has_unlocked_council_positions < 5 civics_count >= 3 } } } set_council_agenda = agenda_unlock_slot }
		add_council_agenda_progress_percent = 1
		if = { limit = { or = { country_uses_consumer_goods = yes has_origin = origin_fear_of_the_dark } } root.capital_scope = { add_building = building_factory_1 } }
		if = { limit = { not = { has_valid_civic = civic_functional_architecture } } force_add_civic = civic_functional_architecture }
	}
	option = {
		name = CHECKBOX_MENU_DONT_SHOW_AGAIN
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_cheat_in_progress
		set_global_flag = daoyu_cheat_dont_show_again
	}
	option = {
		name = CLOSE
		default_hide_option = yes
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_cheat_in_progress
	}
}

#改革政府
country_event = {
	id = daoyu.109
	title = MOD_GOVERNMENT_TITLE
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			text = daoyu_cheat
			if = { limit = { has_distar = yes } text = daoyu_lgate_result_show }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_country_government_civic_points_add_multiplier VALUE_IF_CREATED = 0 }
		export_trigger_value_to_variable = { trigger = resource_stockpile_compare parameters = { resource = unity } variable = daoyu_stockpile_unity }
	}
	option = {
		name = MOD_VETO_COOLDOWN_MULT#否决冷却
		set_government_cooldown = no
	}
	option = {
		name = +1
		custom_tooltip = MOD_COUNTRY_GOVERNMENT_CIVIC_POINTS_ADD
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_modifier = daoyu_country_government_civic_points_add
			change_variable = { which = daoyu_country_government_civic_points_add_multiplier value = 1 }
			add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_country_government_civic_points_add days = -1 multiplier = daoyu_country_government_civic_points_add_multiplier }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = -1
		trigger = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_country_government_civic_points_add_multiplier value > 0 } }
		custom_tooltip = MOD_COUNTRY_GOVERNMENT_CIVIC_POINTS_ADD
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_modifier = daoyu_country_government_civic_points_add
			change_variable = { which = daoyu_country_government_civic_points_add_multiplier value = -1 }
			add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_country_government_civic_points_add days = -1 multiplier = daoyu_country_government_civic_points_add_multiplier }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = r_unity
		add_resource = { unity = 1000 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = daoyu.100 }
			add_resource = { unity = -10000 }
			add_resource = { unity = -1 mult = daoyu_stockpile_unity }
			clear_variable = daoyu_stockpile_unity
		}
	}
	after = { hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back } else = { country_event = { id = daoyu.109 } } } }
}
#限制开关
country_event = {
	id = daoyu.108
	title = daoyu_toggle_restrictions
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = { text = ADD has_global_flag = daoyu_add_global_flag }
			success_text = { text = REMOVE has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_global_flag }
			success_text = { text = newline or = { has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_global_flag has_global_flag = daoyu_add_global_flag } }
			text = USED
			success_text = { text = AMOUNT_NONE daoyu_has_restriction_flag_trigger = no }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_can_excavate_outside_borders has_global_flag = daoyu_can_excavate_outside_borders }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_ai_can_not_build_starbase has_global_flag = daoyu_ai_can_not_build_starbase }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = ADD#添加

		set_global_flag = daoyu_add_global_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = REMOVE#移除
		trigger = { daoyu_has_restriction_flag_trigger = yes nor = { has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_global_flag has_global_flag = daoyu_add_global_flag } }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_remove_global_flag
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_can_excavate_outside_borders#允许发掘无主恒星系的考古遗址
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_global_flag }
		allow = { daoyu_remove_global_flag_trigger = { FLAG = daoyu_can_excavate_outside_borders } }
		daoyu_add_or_remove_global_flag_effect = { FLAG = daoyu_can_excavate_outside_borders }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_can_excavate_outside_borders#允许发掘无主恒星系的考古遗址
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_add_global_flag }
		allow = { daoyu_add_global_flag_trigger = { FLAG = daoyu_can_excavate_outside_borders } }
		daoyu_add_or_remove_global_flag_effect = { FLAG = daoyu_can_excavate_outside_borders }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_ai_can_not_build_starbase#禁止AI建造恒星基地
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_global_flag }
		allow = { daoyu_remove_global_flag_trigger = { FLAG = daoyu_ai_can_not_build_starbase } }
		daoyu_add_or_remove_global_flag_effect = { FLAG = daoyu_ai_can_not_build_starbase }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_ai_can_not_build_starbase#禁止AI建造恒星基地
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_add_global_flag }
		allow = { daoyu_add_global_flag_trigger = { FLAG = daoyu_ai_can_not_build_starbase } }

	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back }
				remove_global_flag = daoyu_back
				if = { limit = { nor = { has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_global_flag has_global_flag = daoyu_add_global_flag } } country_event = { id = daoyu.100 } }
				else = { remove_global_flag = daoyu_remove_global_flag remove_global_flag = daoyu_add_global_flag country_event = { id = daoyu.108 } }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = daoyu.108 } }
		}

	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_hyperlane#创建航路
		set_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A } set_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B country_event = { id = daoyu.114 } }
			else = { country_event = { id = daoyu.111 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_hyperlane#删除航路
		set_global_flag = daoyu_remove_hyperlane
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A }
				daoyu_clear_target_20_effect = yes
				set_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B
				every_system = { limit = { has_hyperlane_to = event_target:daoyu_point_A } set_star_flag = daoyu_potential_target }
				country_event = { id = daoyu.115 }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = daoyu.111 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_select_point_A#选择航路出发地
		trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map } }
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_A
		set_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.114 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map } }
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_A
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_B
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B_on_map
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_remove_hyperlane
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.10 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CLOSE
		default_hide_option = yes
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map }
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_A
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_B
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B_on_map
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_remove_hyperlane
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B
	}

#超空间航道
country_event = {
	id = daoyu.111
	title = concept_hyperlanes
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = { text = daoyu_create_hyperlane has_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_remove_hyperlane has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_hyperlane }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_point_A exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_point_B exists = event_target:daoyu_point_B }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = daoyu_select_point_A#选择航路出发地
		trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map } }
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_A
		set_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.114 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_select_point_B#选择航目的地
		trigger = { or = { has_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A } }
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_B
		set_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane } country_event = { id = daoyu.114 } }
			else = { daoyu_clear_target_20_effect = yes every_system = { limit = { has_hyperlane_to = event_target:daoyu_point_A } set_star_flag = daoyu_potential_target } country_event = { id = daoyu.115 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_hyperlane_confirm#建立超空间连接
		trigger = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A exists = event_target:daoyu_point_B has_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B_on_map } }
		add_hyperlane = { from = event_target:daoyu_point_A to = event_target:daoyu_point_B }
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_B
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.110 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = feature_wormhole_stabilization#虫洞航行
		trigger = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A exists = event_target:daoyu_point_B has_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B_on_map } }
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_point_A = { has_natural_wormhole = no } event_target:daoyu_point_B = { has_natural_wormhole = no } }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.113 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_hyperlane_confirm#删除超空间连接
		trigger = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A exists = event_target:daoyu_point_B has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_hyperlane }
		remove_hyperlane = { from = event_target:daoyu_point_A to = event_target:daoyu_point_B }
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_B
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_remove_hyperlane
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map } clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_A remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map }
			else = { country_event = { id = daoyu.110 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		if = { limit = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map } } clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_A }
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_B
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_remove_hyperlane
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.110 } }
	}
}

	desc = daoyu_wormhole_cannot_be_deleted
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_wormhole#确认
		if = { limit = { not = { has_country_flag = encountered_first_wormhole } } set_country_flag = encountered_first_wormhole }
		if = { limit = { not = { has_seen_any_bypass = wormhole } } add_seen_bypass_type = wormhole }
		if = { limit = { nor = { has_tech_option = tech_hyper_drive_2 has_technology = tech_hyper_drive_2 } } add_research_option = tech_hyper_drive_2 }
		if = { limit = { nor = { has_tech_option = tech_wormhole_stabilization has_technology = tech_wormhole_stabilization } } add_research_option = tech_wormhole_stabilization }
		hidden_effect = {
			event_target:daoyu_point_A = { spawn_natural_wormhole = { bypass_type = wormhole random_pos = no orbit_angle = 360 } set_star_flag = daoyu_has_wormhole }
			event_target:daoyu_point_B = { spawn_natural_wormhole = { bypass_type = wormhole random_pos = no orbit_angle = 270 } link_wormholes = event_target:daoyu_point_A }
			clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_A
			clear_global_event_target = daoyu_point_B
			remove_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map } remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map }
			else = { country_event = { id = daoyu.110 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.111 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = daoyu.114
	title = concept_hyperlanes
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = { text = daoyu_create_hyperlane has_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_remove_hyperlane has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_hyperlane }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_point_A has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_point_B has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A exists = event_target:daoyu_point_B }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_select_point_A has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_select_point_B has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { every_system = { limit = { has_star_flag = daoyu_potential_target } remove_star_flag = daoyu_potential_target } }
	option = {
		name = daoyu_select_point_B_on_map#在星球决议中选择航路目的地
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map has_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B_on_map
		daoyu_special_project_select_target = yes
		custom_tooltip = daoyu_pause_game
	}
	option = {
		name = holy_war_1_poi#首都恒星系
		trigger = {
			or = {
				and = {
					has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A
					or = {
						and = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_B event_target:daoyu_point_B = { nor = { is_same_value = root.capital_scope.solar_system has_hyperlane_to = capital_scope.solar_system } } }
						not = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_B }
					}
				}
				and = {
					has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B
					or = {
						and = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A event_target:daoyu_point_A = { nor = { is_same_value = root.capital_scope.solar_system has_hyperlane_to = capital_scope.solar_system } } }
						not = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		root.capital_scope.solar_system = { daoyu_select_point_A_or_point_B_effect = yes }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_located_shipclass_science_ship#科研船所在的星系
		trigger = { daoyu_select_point_A_or_point_B_trigger = { CLASS = shipclass_science_ship } }
		daoyu_select_potential_point_A_or_point_B_effect = { CLASS = shipclass_science_ship }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_located_shipclass_constructor#工程船所在的星系
		trigger = { daoyu_select_point_A_or_point_B_trigger = { CLASS = shipclass_constructor } }
		daoyu_select_potential_point_A_or_point_B_effect = { CLASS = shipclass_constructor }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_located_shipclass_colonizer#殖民船所在的星系
		trigger = { daoyu_select_point_A_or_point_B_trigger = { CLASS = shipclass_colonizer } }
		daoyu_select_potential_point_A_or_point_B_effect = { CLASS = shipclass_colonizer }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_located_shipclass_transport#运输船所在的星系
		trigger = { daoyu_select_point_A_or_point_B_trigger = { CLASS = shipclass_transport } }
		daoyu_select_potential_point_A_or_point_B_effect = { CLASS = shipclass_transport }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_located_shipclass_military#军事船所在的星系
		trigger = { daoyu_select_point_A_or_point_B_trigger = { CLASS = shipclass_military } }
		daoyu_select_potential_point_A_or_point_B_effect = { CLASS = shipclass_military }
	}
	option = {
		name = ANY_NEIGHBOR_SYSTEM#任意邻近恒星系
		trigger = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A }
		daoyu_clear_target_20_effect = yes
		every_system = {
			limit = {
				nor = { is_same_value = event_target:daoyu_point_A has_hyperlane_to = event_target:daoyu_point_A }
				distance = { source = event_target:daoyu_point_A type = euclidean min_distance >= 0 max_distance <= 30 }
			}
			set_star_flag = daoyu_potential_target
		}
		set_variable = { which = daoyu_euclidean_distance value = 30 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B_on_map } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map has_global_flag = daoyu_back exists = { event_target:daoyu_point_B } } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back country_event = { id = daoyu.111 } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back country_event = { id = daoyu.110 } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back country_event = { id = daoyu.111 } }
			else = { country_event = { id = daoyu.115 } }
		}
	}
}

				else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A nor = { has_global_flag = daoyu_create_hyperlane has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_hyperlane } } remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A country_event = { id = daoyu.110 } }

				else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B exists = event_target:daoyu_point_B } clear_variable = daoyu_euclidean_distance remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B country_event = { id = daoyu.111 } }
				else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A not = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_A } } country_event = { id = daoyu.114 } }
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_hyperlane has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_A_on_map not = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_B } }
					remove_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B country_event = { id = daoyu.111 }
				}
				else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_select_point_B not = { exists = event_target:daoyu_point_B } } country_event = { id = daoyu.114 } }
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = daoyu_hyperlane_AI_recovery#恢复AI到境外的超空间链接

		remove_global_flag = daoyu_hyperlane_AI_remove
		set_global_flag = daoyu_hyperlane_AI_recovery
		daoyu_99_num = yes
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_hyperlane_AI_recovery
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.116 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.110 } }
	}

#设置
country_event = {
	id = daoyu.131
	title = SETTINGS#设置
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			text = ACTIVE_STAGE
			text = newline
			success_text = { text = daoyu_random_existing_design has_global_flag = daoyu_random_existing_design }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_cheat_design has_global_flag = daoyu_cheat_design }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_leviathan_design has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design }
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design has_global_flag = daoyu_friendly_fleets } text = daoyu_friendly_fleets }
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design has_global_flag = daoyu_neutral_fleets } text = daoyu_neutral_fleets }
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design has_global_flag = daoyu_hostile_fleets } text = daoyu_hostile_fleets }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design } } text = newline }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_all_x1 has_global_flag = daoyu_all_x1 not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design } }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_all_x5 has_global_flag = daoyu_all_x5 not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design } }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_all_x10 has_global_flag = daoyu_all_x10 not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design } }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_all_x100 has_global_flag = daoyu_all_x100 not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design } }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_all_x1000 has_global_flag = daoyu_all_x1000 not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design } }
			if = { limit = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design } } text = newline }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_assign_leader_after_event has_global_flag = daoyu_assign_leader_after_event not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design } }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_no_leader_after_event has_global_flag = daoyu_no_leader_after_event not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_leviathan_design } }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = event_target:daoyu_target_planet
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = daoyu_random_existing_design#随机已存在的设计

country_event = {
	id = daoyu.140
	title = daoyu_dlc_biogenesis
	desc = daoyu_cheat
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = anomaly.3135.name#保持冷静
		allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = ACTIVE_RESOLUTION any_owned_ship = { or = { is_ship_size = behemoth_01 is_ship_size = behemoth_02 is_ship_size = behemoth_03 is_ship_size = behemoth_04 } not = { has_ship_flag = daoyu_recently_fed } } } }
		every_owned_ship = { limit = { or = { is_ship_size = behemoth_01 is_ship_size = behemoth_02 is_ship_size = behemoth_03 is_ship_size = behemoth_04 } } remove_ship_flag = recently_fed set_ship_flag = recently_fed set_ship_flag = daoyu_recently_fed }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.140 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = bioship_growth#生物舰船生长
		allow = { any_owned_ship = { or = { is_ship_size = behemoth_01 is_ship_size = behemoth_02 is_ship_size = behemoth_03 } } }
		every_owned_ship = { limit = { or = { is_ship_size = behemoth_01 is_ship_size = behemoth_02 is_ship_size = behemoth_03 } } add_growth = 1000 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.140 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = MULTIPLE_SHIPS_DISBAND_TITLE#解散舰船
		allow = {
			any_owned_ship = { or = { is_ship_size = behemoth_01 is_ship_size = behemoth_02 is_ship_size = behemoth_03 is_ship_size = behemoth_04 } }
			custom_tooltip = { fail_text = RESEARCH_PROJECT_ORDER not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_fleets_disband_special_project } }
		}
		set_global_flag = daoyu_fleets_disband_special_project daoyu_special_project_select_target = yes
		custom_tooltip = RESEARCH_PROJECT_ORDER
		custom_tooltip = daoyu_pause_game
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.140 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.10 } }
	}

#舰队传送
country_event = {
	id = daoyu.150
	title = daoyu_fleet_teleportation
	desc = daoyu_pause_game
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = from
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { event_target:daoyu_teleportation_fleet = { clear_orders = yes set_location = from } clear_global_event_target = daoyu_teleportation_fleet }
	option = {
		name = shipclass_science_ship#科研船
		trigger = { any_controlled_fleet = { is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship } }
		if = { limit = { count_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship } count > 1 } } every_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship } set_fleet_flag = daoyu_potential_target } }
		else = { custom_tooltip = daoyu_special_project_select_target random_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_science_ship } save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_teleportation_fleet } }
	}
	option = {
		name = shipclass_constructor#工程船
		trigger = { any_controlled_fleet = { is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor } }
		if = { limit = { count_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor } count > 1 } } every_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor } set_fleet_flag = daoyu_potential_target } }
		else = { custom_tooltip = daoyu_special_project_select_target random_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_constructor } save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_teleportation_fleet } }
	}
	option = {
		name = shipclass_colonizer#殖民船
		trigger = { any_controlled_fleet = { is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer } }
		if = { limit = { count_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer } count > 1 } } every_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer } set_fleet_flag = daoyu_potential_target } }
		else = { custom_tooltip = daoyu_special_project_select_target random_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_colonizer } save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_teleportation_fleet } }
	}
	option = {
		name = shipclass_transport#运输船
		trigger = { any_controlled_fleet = { is_ship_class = shipclass_transport } }
		if = { limit = { count_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_transport } count > 1 } } every_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_transport } set_fleet_flag = daoyu_potential_target } }
		else = { custom_tooltip = daoyu_special_project_select_target random_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_transport } save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_teleportation_fleet } }
	}
	option = {
		name = shipclass_military#军事船
		trigger = { any_controlled_fleet = { is_ship_class = shipclass_military } }
		if = { limit = { count_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_military } count > 1 } } every_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_military } set_fleet_flag = daoyu_potential_target } }
		else = { custom_tooltip = daoyu_special_project_select_target random_controlled_fleet = { limit = { is_ship_class = shipclass_military } save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_teleportation_fleet } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_teleportation_fleet
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.10 } }
	}
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { exists = event_target:daoyu_teleportation_fleet }
			save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_root
			every_system = {
				limit = { not = { any_fleet_in_system = { is_same_value = event_target:daoyu_teleportation_fleet } } or = { not = { exists = space_owner } and = { exists = space_owner space_owner = { is_same_value = root } } } }
				every_system_planet = { limit = { is_surveyed = { who = root status = yes } not = { exists = owner } or = { is_colonizable = no solar_system = { not = { exists = space_owner } } } } hidden_effect = { planet_event = { id = daoyu_common.20 } } }
			}
		}
		else_if = { limit = { any_controlled_fleet = { has_fleet_flag = daoyu_potential_target } } hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.151 } } }
	}
}
