			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier } text = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier } text = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier } text = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier } text = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_empire_size_modifier } text = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier } text = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_planet_modifier } text = daoyu_planet_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_1 } text = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_1 }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_2 } text = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_2 }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_3 } text = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_3 }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = ADD#添加
		set_global_flag = daoyu_add_modifiers
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.191 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = DELETE#删除
		allow = { daoyu_has_country_modifiers = yes }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.195 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CDV_RESET#重置
		allow = { daoyu_has_country_modifiers = yes }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.199 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.100 } }
	}
}
#帝国修正
country_event = {
	id = daoyu.191
	title = daoyu_add_modifiers
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			itext = daoyu_can_add_modifiers_multiple_times
			text = ACTIVE_MODIFIERS
			if = { limit = { daoyu_has_country_modifiers = no } text = SECTOR_SHARE_NONE }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier } text = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_research_speed_modifier } text = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier } text = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier } text = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier } text = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier } text = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier } text = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_empire_size_modifier } text = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier } text = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_planet_modifier } text = daoyu_planet_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_1 } text = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_1 }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_2 } text = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_2 }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_3 } text = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_3 }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_var VALUE_IF_CREATED = 1 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var VALUE_IF_CREATED = 20 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var VALUE_IF_CREATED = 20 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var VALUE_IF_CREATED = 20 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_var VALUE_IF_CREATED = 5 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier_var VALUE_IF_CREATED = 1 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_var VALUE_IF_CREATED = -1 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_var VALUE_IF_CREATED = -1 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_var VALUE_IF_CREATED = 1 }
		create_variable_if_not_exists = { VARIABLE = daoyu_planet_modifier_var VALUE_IF_CREATED = 1 }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier#备选科技
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_var value = 0 } } } set_variable = { which = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_show value = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_var } } }
		add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier days = -1 multiplier = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_var }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_var value < 5 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_var value = 1 } }
			else = { change_variable = { which = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_var value = 5 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_research_speed_modifier#研究速度
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var value = 0 } } } set_variable = { which = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_show value = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var } } }
		add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_research_speed_modifier days = -1 multiplier = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var value < 100 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var value = 20 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var value < 1000 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var value = 100 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var value < 10000 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var value = 1000 } }
			else = { multiply_variable = { which = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var value = 2 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier#建筑速度
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var value = 0 } } } set_variable = { which = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_show value = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var } } }
		add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier days = -1 multiplier = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var value < 100 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var value = 20 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var value < 1000 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var value = 100 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var value < 10000 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var value = 1000 } }
			else = { multiply_variable = { which = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var value = 2 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier#造船速度
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var value = 0 } } } set_variable = { which = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_show value = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var } } }
		add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier days = -1 multiplier = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var value < 100 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var value = 20 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var value < 1000 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var value = 100 } }
			else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var value < 10000 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var value = 1000 } }
			else = { multiply_variable = { which = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var value = 2 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier#善于适应
		trigger = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_show value = 100 } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_var value = 0 } } }
				set_variable = { which = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_show value = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_var }
			}
		}
		add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier days = -1 multiplier = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_var }
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_var value < 100 } } change_variable = { which = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_var value = 5 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier#考古技能
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier_var value = 0 } } } set_variable = { which = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier_show value = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier_var } } }
		add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier days = -1 multiplier = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier_var }
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier_var value = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier#舰船维护费
		trigger = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_show value = -100 } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_var value = 0 } } }
				set_variable = { which = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_show value = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_var }
				multiply_variable = { which = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_show value = 5 }
			}
		}
		add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier days = -1 multiplier = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_var }
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_var value = -1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_empire_size_modifier#帝国规模
		trigger = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_show value = -100 } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_var value = 0 } } }
				set_variable = { which = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_show value = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_var }
				multiply_variable = { which = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_show value = 5 }
			}
		}
		add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_empire_size_modifier days = -1 multiplier = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_var }
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_var value = -1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier#资源储存上限
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_var value = 0 } } }
				set_variable = { which = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_show value = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_var }
				multiply_variable = { which = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_show value = 100000 }
			}
		}
		add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier days = -1 multiplier = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_var }
		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_var value = 1 } }
	}
	option = {

		trigger = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_planet_modifier_show value = 100 } } }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { not = { check_variable = { which = daoyu_planet_modifier_var value = 0 } } }
				set_variable = { which = daoyu_planet_modifier_show value = daoyu_planet_modifier_var }
				multiply_variable = { which = daoyu_planet_modifier_show value = 5 }

		hidden_effect = { change_variable = { which = daoyu_planet_modifier_var value = 1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_military_experience_modifier#初始经验
		trigger = { not = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_3 } }
		if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_2 } hidden_effect = { remove_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_2 } add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_3 days = -1 } }
		else_if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_1 } hidden_effect = { remove_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_1 } add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_2 days = -1 } }
		else = { add_modifier = { modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_1 days = -1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
	}
	after = { hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back country_event = { id = daoyu.190 } } else = { country_event = { id = daoyu.191 } } } }
}

country_event = {
	id = daoyu.199
	title = CDV_RESET#帝国修正
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			text = ACTIVE_MODIFIERS
			if = { limit = { daoyu_has_country_modifiers = no } text = SECTOR_SHARE_NONE }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier } text = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier } text = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_research_speed_modifier } text = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier } text = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier } text = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier } text = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier } text = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier } text = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_empire_size_modifier } text = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier } text = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_planet_modifier } text = daoyu_planet_modifier_desc }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_1 } text = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_1 }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_2 } text = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_2 }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_3 } text = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_3 }
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM#确认
		remove_modifier = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier
		remove_modifier = daoyu_research_speed_modifier
		remove_modifier = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier
		remove_modifier = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier
		remove_modifier = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier
		remove_modifier = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier
		remove_modifier = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier
		remove_modifier = daoyu_empire_size_modifier
		remove_modifier = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier
		remove_modifier = daoyu_planet_modifier
		remove_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_1
		remove_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_2
		remove_modifier = daoyu_military_experience_modifier_3
		hidden_effect = {
			clear_variable = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_var
			clear_variable = daoyu_num_tech_add_modifier_show
			clear_variable = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_var
			clear_variable = daoyu_research_speed_modifier_show
			clear_variable = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_var
			clear_variable = daoyu_building_build_speed_modifier_show
			clear_variable = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_var
			clear_variable = daoyu_ship_build_speed_modifier_show
			clear_variable = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_var
			clear_variable = daoyu_environment_tolerance_modifier_show
			clear_variable = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier_var
			clear_variable = daoyu_archaeological_site_clues_modifier_show
			clear_variable = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_var
			clear_variable = daoyu_upkeep_mult_modifier_show
			clear_variable = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_var
			clear_variable = daoyu_empire_size_modifier_show
			clear_variable = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_var
			clear_variable = daoyu_country_resource_max_add_modifier_show
			clear_variable = daoyu_planet_modifier_var
			clear_variable = daoyu_planet_modifier_show

		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
	after = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.190 } } }
}

#领袖
country_event = {
	id = daoyu.250
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = { text = daoyu_target_leader_councilor_type exists = event_target:daoyu_target_leader }
			success_text = { text = LEADER_ASSIGNMENT not = { exists = event_target:daoyu_target_leader } }
			text = newline
			success_text = { text = daoyu_show_more_trait exists = event_target:daoyu_target_leader has_global_flag = daoyu_show_more_trait }
			success_text = { text = daoyu_show_default_trait exists = event_target:daoyu_target_leader not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_show_more_trait } }
		}
	}
	show_sound = event_custodian_greeting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_leader_recruitment_bg_renowned
	event_window_type = leader_recruit
	notification_event_icon = "GFX_message_leader_recruitment_lysator"
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:daoyu_target_leader
		room = ethic_spaceship_room
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_all_negative_traits#删除负面特质
		trigger = { or = { any_owned_leader = { num_leader_traits = { value > 0 negative = yes } } any_pool_leader = { num_leader_traits = { value > 0 negative = yes } } } }
		every_owned_leader = { limit = { num_leader_traits = { value > 0 negative = yes } } daoyu_remove_all_negative_traits = yes }
		every_pool_leader = { limit = { num_leader_traits = { value > 0 negative = yes } } daoyu_remove_all_negative_traits = yes }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.250 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_leader_template#领袖模板
		trigger = { or = { daoyu_has_template_leader = yes exists = event_target:daoyu_target_leader } }
		allow = { or = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = daoyu_saved_leader daoyu_has_template_leader = yes } custom_tooltip = { fail_text = LEADER_ASSIGNMENT exists = event_target:daoyu_target_leader } } }
		hidden_effect = { if = { limit = { exists = event_target:daoyu_target_leader } country_event = { id = daoyu.252 } } else = { country_event = { id = daoyu.255 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = LEADER_SELECTION#选择领袖
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_target_leader
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.260 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_leader_traits#领袖特质
		allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = LEADER_ASSIGNMENT exists = event_target:daoyu_target_leader } }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_add_trait
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.270 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_leader_ethic#领袖思潮
		allow = { is_gestalt = no }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_ethic_from_leader
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_ethic.1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_leader_age#领袖年龄
		allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = LEADER_ASSIGNMENT exists = event_target:daoyu_target_leader } }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_ethic_from_leader
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.257 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_free_leader#领袖免费
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_leader = { or = { is_gestalt = no and = { is_councilor = no is_gestalt = yes } } not = { has_leader_flag = hired_admiral_merc_leader } } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_leader = { set_leader_flag = hired_admiral_merc_leader }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.250 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_cancel_free_leader#领袖免费
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_leader = { has_leader_flag = hired_admiral_merc_leader } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_leader = { remove_leader_flag = hired_admiral_merc_leader }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.250 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = UPGRADE#升级
		tag = hire_leader
		allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = LEADER_ASSIGNMENT exists = event_target:daoyu_target_leader } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_leader = { add_skill = 1 }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.250 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		tag = dismiss_leader
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_show_more_trait
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_target_leader
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.10 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = daoyu.252
	desc = daoyu_template_leader_desc
	show_sound = event_custodian_greeting
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_leader_recruitment_bg_renowned
	event_window_type = leader_recruit
	notification_event_icon = "GFX_message_leader_recruitment_lysator"
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:daoyu_target_leader
		room = ethic_spaceship_room
	}
	option = {
		name = SAVE#保存
		allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = daoyu_current_leader_has_veteran_trait exists = event_target:daoyu_target_leader event_target:daoyu_target_leader = { num_leader_traits = { value > 0 is_subclass = yes } } } }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_save_leader
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.253 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = DELETE#删除
		allow = {
			custom_tooltip = {
				fail_text = daoyu_saved_leader#存在已保存的领袖
				daoyu_has_template_leader = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.253 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_clone_leader#克隆领袖
		event_target:daoyu_target_leader = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_view_template_leader }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.255 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ESPIONAGE_IS_UNAVAILABLE#不可用
		tag = hire_leader
		allow = { always = no }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		tag = dismiss_leader
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.250 } }
	}
}

			success_text = { text = daoyu_show_more_trait and = { has_global_flag = daoyu_add_trait has_global_flag = daoyu_show_more_trait } }
		}
	}
	show_sound = event_custodian_greeting
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = daoyu_remove_all_negative_traits#删除负面特质

		event_target:daoyu_target_leader = { daoyu_remove_all_negative_traits = yes }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.270 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_add_trait#添加特质
		allow = { has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_trait }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_remove_trait
		set_global_flag = daoyu_add_trait
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.270 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_trait#删除特质
		allow = { has_global_flag = daoyu_add_trait }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_add_trait
		set_global_flag = daoyu_remove_trait
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.270 } }
	}

		set_global_flag = daoyu_remove_all_negative_traits
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.301 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_all_empire_species_chenge_to_owner_main_species#所有帝国物种变为主体物种
		trigger = { count_owned_species = { count > 1 } }
		allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = daoyu_cooldown_1 not = { has_country_flag = daoyu_all_empire_species_chenge_to_owner_main_species_cooldown } } }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_all_empire_species_chenge_to_owner_main_species
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.301 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = SPECIES_SELECT_TITLE#选择物种
		allow = { custom_tooltip = { fail_text = daoyu_cooldown_1 not = { has_country_flag = daoyu_select_species_cooldown } } }
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_target_species
		daoyu_clear_target_20_species_effect = yes
		set_country_flag = daoyu_select_species
		set_timed_country_flag = { flag = daoyu_select_species_cooldown days = 1 }
		if = { limit = { count_owned_species = { count > 1 } } every_owned_species = { set_species_flag = daoyu_potential_target } hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.302 } } }
		else = { daoyu_save_pop_citizenship_effect = yes random_owned_species = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_species } hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.303 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.10 } }
	}
}

				country_event = { id = daoyu.303 }
			}
			else = { every_owned_species = { limit = { has_species_flag = daoyu_potential_target } remove_species_flag = daoyu_potential_target } remove_country_flag = daoyu_select_species country_event = { id = daoyu.10 } }
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = daoyu.303
	title = species_traits_editor#物种特质
	desc = daoyu_target_species
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	location = capital_scope
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_all_negative_traits#删除负面特质
		trigger = { event_target:daoyu_target_species = { daoyu_pop_has_negative_traits = yes } }
		daoyu_target_species_remove_negative_traits = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.303 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = buildable_colony_ship#建造殖民船
		create_fleet = { effect = { set_owner = root create_ship = { random_existing_design = colonizer colonizer_species = event_target:daoyu_target_species graphical_culture = root } set_location = root.capital_scope } }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.303 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = PLANET_CLASS_PREFERENCE_TRAITS#行星偏好
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_target_species = { not = { has_trait = trait_pc_habitat_preference has_trait = trait_void_dweller_1 } } }
		custom_tooltip = trait_aquatic custom_tooltip = trait_robot_aquatic custom_tooltip = trait_void_dweller_1 custom_tooltip = SPECIAL_PROJECT_STATUS_UNAVAILABLE
		if = { limit = { event_target:daoyu_target_species = { or = { has_trait = trait_aquatic has_trait = trait_void_dweller_1 has_trait = trait_robot_aquatic } } } hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.303 } } }
		else = {
			if = { limit = { event_target:daoyu_target_species = { or = { is_archetype = BIOLOGICAL is_archetype = PRESAPIENT is_archetype = LITHOID } } } hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.304 } } }
			if = { limit = { event_target:daoyu_target_species = { or = { is_archetype = MACHINE is_archetype = ROBOT } } } hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.305 } } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_add_trait#添加特质
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_species_traits.1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_trait#删除特质
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_species_traits.2 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_special_trait#删除特殊特质
		trigger = {
			event_target:daoyu_target_species = {
				or = {
					has_trait = trait_hive_mind has_trait = trait_machine_unit has_trait = trait_mechanical has_trait = trait_lithoid has_trait = trait_necrophage has_trait = trait_zombie has_trait = trait_limited_cybernetic
					has_trait = trait_cybernetic has_trait = trait_uplifted has_trait = trait_enigmatic_intelligence has_trait = trait_enigmatic_intelligence_poor has_trait = trait_enigmatic_intelligence_failed has_trait = trait_latent_psionic
					has_trait = trait_psionic has_trait = trait_clone_soldier_infertile has_trait = trait_clone_soldier_infertile_full_potential has_trait = trait_clone_soldier_fertile has_trait = trait_cave_dweller
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_species_traits.3 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_change_dominant_species
		trigger = { owner_main_species = { not = { is_same_value = event_target:daoyu_target_species } } }
		change_dominant_species = { species = event_target:daoyu_target_species }
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.303 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = ETHIC#思潮
		set_global_flag = daoyu_species_pop_group_transfer_ethic
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu_ethic.1 } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		species = { modify_species = { species = event_target:daoyu_target_species change_scoped_species = yes } }
		if = { limit = { count_owned_species = { count > 1 } } daoyu_restore_pop_citizenship_effect = yes remove_country_flag = daoyu_select_species }
		clear_global_event_target = daoyu_target_species
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.10 } }
	}
}

	option = {
		name = NEXT
		trigger = { any_country = { has_country_flag = daoyu_potential_target } }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_refresh
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
		every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = daoyu_potential_target } remove_country_flag = daoyu_potential_target }
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
	after = {
		daoyu_clear_target_20_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_refresh } remove_global_flag = daoyu_refresh country_event = { id = daoyu.802 } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back country_event = { id = daoyu.800 } }
			else = { every_country = { limit = { has_country_flag = daoyu_potential_target } remove_country_flag = daoyu_potential_target } add_intel = { who = event_target:daoyu_target_country amount = 10 } country_event = { id = daoyu.803 } }
		}
	}
}

#换国家
country_event = {
	id = daoyu.804
	title = daoyu_target_country
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = { text = daoyu_play_as_target_country has_global_flag = daoyu_play_as_target_country }
			success_text = { text = FLEET_MANAGER_DELETE_TEMPLATE_DIALOG_TITLE has_global_flag = daoyu_target_country_delete_fleet }
			success_text = { text = operation_steal_technology has_global_flag = daoyu_copy_techs_from_target_country }
			success_text = { text = distar.3021.name has_global_flag = daoyu_target_country_copy_techs_from_root }
			success_text = { text = MAKE_CLAIMS has_global_flag = daoyu_add_claims_target_country }
		}
	}
	diplomatic = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	custom_gui = "formless_diplomacy_window"
	location = event_target:daoyu_target_country.capital_scope
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = event_target:daoyu_target_country.ruler
		planet_background = event_target:daoyu_target_country.owner
		graphical_culture = event_target:daoyu_target_country.owner
		city_level = event_target:daoyu_target_country.owner
		room = event_target:daoyu_target_country.owner
	}
	immediate = { set_global_flag = daoyu_back }
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_play_as_target_country }
		event_target:daoyu_target_country = { set_player = root }
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_cheat_in_progress
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_back
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_target_country_delete_fleet }
		allow = { event_target:daoyu_target_country = { is_primitive = no count_controlled_fleet = { limit = { or = { is_ship_class = shipclass_military is_ship_class = shipclass_transport } } count > 0 } } }
		event_target:daoyu_target_country = {
			every_controlled_fleet = { limit = { not = { is_ship_class = shipclass_starbase } or = { is_ship_class = shipclass_military is_ship_class = shipclass_transport } } delete_fleet = this }
			every_system_within_border = { starbase = { if = { limit = { not = { has_starbase_size = starbase_outpost } } set_starbase_size = starbase_outpost } } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_copy_techs_from_target_country }
		copy_techs_from = { target = event_target:daoyu_target_country }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_target_country_copy_techs_from_root }
		event_target:daoyu_target_country = { copy_techs_from = { target = root } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_add_claims_target_country }
		every_system = {
			limit = { is_owned_by = event_target:daoyu_target_country not = { root = { has_claim = prev } } }
			if = { limit = { any_system_planet = { is_surveyed = { who = root status = yes } } } add_claims = { who = root show_notification = no } }
			else = { root = { set_visited = prev } random_system_planet = { limit = { is_star = yes } set_surveyed = { surveyed = yes surveyor = root } } }
		}
		if = { limit = { any_system = { is_owned_by = event_target:daoyu_target_country not = { any_system_planet = { is_surveyed = { who = root status = yes } } } } } event_target:daoyu_target_country = { country_event = { id = daoyu.805 days = 1 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
	after = {
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_play_as_target_country
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_target_country_delete_fleet
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_copy_techs_from_target_country
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_target_country_copy_techs_from_root
		remove_global_flag = daoyu_add_claims_target_country
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = daoyu.803 } }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = daoyu.900
	title = AUTO_GENERATED_STANDARD
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			success_text = { text = ADD has_global_flag = daoyu_add_global_flag }
			success_text = { text = REMOVE has_global_flag = daoyu_remove_global_flag }

country_event = {
	id = daoyu.902
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		#删除负面特质
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_auto_remove_leader_negative_traits } every_owned_leader = { daoyu_remove_all_negative_traits = yes } }
		#考古遗迹建哨站
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_auto_build_outpost_at_arc_site }
			every_galaxy_planet = {
				limit = { not = { has_planet_flag = daoyu_has_build_outpost_at_arc_site } daoyu_has_archaeological_site_trigger = yes solar_system = { has_owner = no not = { any_system_planet = { is_surveyed = { who = root status = no } } } } }
				if = { limit = { has_planet_flag = daoyu_auto_build_outpost_at_arc_site_dont_show_again } set_planet_flag = daoyu_has_build_outpost_at_arc_site solar_system = { create_starbase = { size = starbase_outpost owner = root } } }
				else = { random_country = { limit = { is_ai = no } country_event = { id = daoyu.910 scopes = { from = prev } } } }
			}
		}
		#考古遗迹增加线索
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_auto_excavate_site_add_stage_clues }
			every_archaeological_site = { limit = { any_galaxy_fleet = { is_owned_by = root prev = { is_current_excavator_fleet = prev } } } add_stage_clues = 100 }
		}
		#第一次接触增加线索
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_auto_first_contact_add_stage_clues }
			every_first_contact = { limit = { contact_country = { or = { is_capturable_space_critter_country_type = yes daoyu_has_enclave_trigger = yes is_country_type = enclave_mercenary } } } add_stage_clues = 100 }
		}
		#未宣称的星系建哨站
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_auto_build_outpost_at_unclaimed }
			every_system = {
				limit = { has_owner = no not = { any_system_planet = { is_surveyed = { who = root status = no } } } }
				create_starbase = { size = starbase_outpost owner = root }
			}
		}
		#建造开采站研究站
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_auto_build_mining_or_research_station }
			every_planet_within_border = { limit = { daoyu_can_build_mining_station_trigger = yes } create_mining_station = { owner = root } }
			every_planet_within_border = { limit = { daoyu_can_build_research_station_trigger = yes } create_research_station = { owner = root } }
		}
		#建造超空间中继器
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_auto_build_hyper_relay }
			every_system_within_border = {
				if = { limit = { any_system_megastructure = { is_megastructure_type = hyper_relay_ruined } } random_system_megastructure = { limit = { is_megastructure_type = hyper_relay_ruined } remove_megastructure = this } }
				if = { limit = { nor = { has_megastructure = hyper_relay_restored has_megastructure = hyper_relay } } spawn_megastructure = { type = "hyper_relay" random_pos = yes orbit_angle = 360 owner = root graphical_culture = root } }
			}
		}
		#缓解资源短缺
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_auto_reduce_resource_scarcity } daoyu_reduce_resource_scarcity_effect = yes }
		#自动统一思想
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_auto_seek_unity_of_ethic } daoyu_auto_seek_unity_of_ethic_effect = yes }
		#免费领袖
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_auto_free_leader }
			every_owned_leader = { limit = { not = { has_leader_flag = hired_admiral_merc_leader } } set_leader_flag = hired_admiral_merc_leader }
		}
		#特殊项目
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_auto_project_complete } daoyu_auto_project_complete_effect = yes }
	}
}

	option = { name = daoyu_target_14 trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_target_14 } event_target:daoyu_target_14 = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_situation } }
	option = { name = daoyu_target_15 trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_target_15 } event_target:daoyu_target_15 = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_situation } }
	option = { name = daoyu_target_16 trigger = { has_global_flag = daoyu_target_16 } event_target:daoyu_target_16 = { save_global_event_target_as = daoyu_target_situation } }

	option = {

		trigger = { any_situation = { has_situation_flag = daoyu_potential_target } }
		set_global_flag = daoyu_refresh
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		set_global_flag = daoyu_back
		every_situation = { limit = { has_situation_flag = daoyu_potential_target } remove_situation_flag = daoyu_potential_target }
		default_hide_option = yes
	}
	after = {
		daoyu_clear_target_20_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_refresh } remove_global_flag = daoyu_refresh country_event = { id = daoyu.950 } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back } remove_global_flag = daoyu_back country_event = { id = daoyu.100 } }
			else = { every_situation = { limit = { has_situation_flag = daoyu_potential_target } remove_situation_flag = daoyu_potential_target } event_target:daoyu_target_situation = { situation_event = { id = daoyu.951 } } }
		}
	}
}

situation_event = {
	id = daoyu.951
	title = situations
	desc = daoyu_situation_desc
	picture = GFX_evt_daoyu_cheat
	show_sound = event_mystic_reveal
	is_triggered_only = yes
	situation = this
	force_open = yes
	option = { name = +1000 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = 1000 }
	option = { name = +500 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = 500 }
	option = { name = +100 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = 100 }
	option = { name = +50 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = 50 }
	option = { name = +10 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = 10 }
	option = { name = +5 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = 5 }
	option = { name = +1 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = 1 }
	option = { name = -1 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = -1 }
	option = { name = -5 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = -5 }
	option = { name = -10 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = -10 }
	option = { name = -50 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = -50 }
	option = { name = -100 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = -100 }
	option = { name = -500 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = -500 }
	option = { name = -1000 trigger = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } add_situation_progress = -1000 }
	option = {
		name = REMOVE#移除
		if = { limit = { not = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } } set_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation }
		else = { set_timed_situation_flag = { flag = daoyu_remove_situation days = 1 } destroy_situation = this remove_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation set_global_flag = daoyu_back }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_back
		default_hide_option = yes
		if = { limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation } remove_global_flag = daoyu_destroy_situation }
		else = { clear_global_event_target = daoyu_target_situation set_global_flag = daoyu_back }
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = daoyu_back }
				remove_global_flag = daoyu_back
				owner = { if = { limit = { daoyu_has_any_situation_trigger = yes } country_event = { id = daoyu.950 } } else = { country_event = { id = daoyu.10 } } }
			}
			else = { situation_event = { id = daoyu.951 } }
		}
	}
}
